### [1] [Symmetrizing Bregman Divergence on the Cone of Positive Definite Matrices: Which Mean to Use and Why](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28917)
*Tushar Sial,Abhishek Halder*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了在正定矩阵锥上由通用镜像映射诱导的Bregman散度对称化的变分原理，证明了不同对称化方式对应的规范均值计算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Bregman散度在正定矩阵锥上的对称化问题，理解现有文献中对称化实践背后的数学原理，为选择合适的均值提供理论指导。

Method: 通过变分原理分析Bregman散度的对称化，将规范均值的计算表述为在满足特定公理性质的均值泛函集合上最小化对称化散度。分别研究前向对称化和反向对称化两种情况。

Result: 1. 对于前向对称化，任何镜像映射在正定锥上的规范均值都是原始空间上的算术平均。
2. 对于反向对称化，规范均值是对偶空间上的算术平均拉回到原始空间。
3. 将结果应用于三种常见镜像映射，得到反向对称化的规范均值分别为算术平均、对数欧几里得平均和调和平均。

Conclusion: 该研究深化了对Bregman散度对称化实践的理解，为选择适当的均值提供了理论依据，可视为帮助决定何时使用何种均值的导航图。

Abstract: This work uncovers variational principles behind symmetrizing the Bregman divergences induced by generic mirror maps over the cone of positive definite matrices. We show that computing the canonical means for this symmetrization can be posed as minimizing the desired symmetrized divergences over a set of mean functionals defined axiomatically to satisfy certain properties. For the forward symmetrization, we prove that the arithmetic mean over the primal space is canonical for any mirror map over the positive definite cone. For the reverse symmetrization, we show that the canonical mean is the arithmetic mean over the dual space, pulled back to the primal space. Applying this result to three common mirror maps used in practice, we show that the canonical means for reverse symmetrization, in those cases, turn out to be the arithmetic, log-Euclidean and harmonic means. Our results improve understanding of existing symmetrization practices in the literature, and can be seen as a navigational chart to help decide which mean to use when.

</details>


### [2] [Multi-fidelity approaches for general constrained Bayesian optimization with application to aircraft design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28987)
*Oihan Cordelier,Youssef Diouane,Nathalie Bartoli,Eric Laurendeau*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的多保真度贝叶斯优化策略，通过同时考虑目标函数和约束信息来选择保真度级别，显著降低了计算成本并提高了约束合规解的数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 飞机设计中的多学科设计优化问题计算成本高昂。现有多保真度模型仅关注目标函数来选择保真度级别，未能充分利用约束信息来进一步优化计算效率。

Method: 提出新颖的多保真度选择策略，同时考虑目标函数和约束信息来决定如何整合不同保真度级别。使用线性涡格法进行气动分析，有限元法进行结构分析，应用于飞机机翼气动结构设计问题。

Result: 在四个分析测试案例中验证了方法的有效性。在有限计算预算下，相比最先进方法，提出的多保真度方法能产生86%到200%更多的约束合规解。

Conclusion: 通过同时利用目标函数和约束信息进行多保真度选择，可以显著降低计算成本而不影响解的最优性，为计算昂贵的多学科设计优化问题提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Aircraft design relies heavily on solving challenging and computationally expensive Multidisciplinary Design Optimization problems. In this context, there has been growing interest in multi-fidelity models for Bayesian optimization to improve the MDO process by balancing computational cost and accuracy through the combination of high- and low-fidelity simulation models, enabling efficient exploration of the design process at a minimal computational effort. In the existing literature, fidelity selection focuses only on the objective function to decide how to integrate multiple fidelity levels, balancing precision and computational cost using variance reduction criteria. In this work, we propose novel multi-fidelity selection strategies. Specifically, we demonstrate how incorporating information from both the objective and the constraints can further reduce computational costs without compromising the optimality of the solution. We validate the proposed multi-fidelity optimization strategy by applying it to four analytical test cases, showcasing its effectiveness. The proposed method is used to efficiently solve a challenging aircraft wing aero-structural design problem. The proposed setting uses a linear vortex lattice method and a finite element method for the aerodynamic and structural analysis respectively. We show that employing our proposed multi-fidelity approach leads to $86\%$ to $200\%$ more constraint compliant solutions given a limited budget compared to the state-of-the-art approach.

</details>


### [3] [H Infinity Minimal Destabilizing Feedback for Vulnerability Analysis and Attack Design of Nonlinear Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28891)
*Gavin Glenn,Emma J. Reid*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文探讨了鲁棒控制理论中的小增益定理如何被恶意攻击者利用来设计最小规模的反馈攻击，以驱动闭环系统失稳，并证明了在攻击增益略微增加时，能保证广泛非线性系统的内部失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鲁棒稳定性设计用于确保系统在建模不确定性下保持稳定，但同样的理论概念可能被攻击者利用来设计恶意反馈攻击。论文旨在分析如何利用鲁棒控制理论构建最小规模的失稳攻击，并研究这些攻击对非线性系统的影响。

Method: 首先详细回顾了鲁棒控制中允许构建最小失稳器的结果，然后利用线性扰动理论在状态空间背景下明确证明：当攻击增益略微增加时，能保证广泛非线性系统的内部失稳。

Result: 最小规模的攻击仅将系统推到稳定性边界，这些攻击不一定能破坏非线性系统的稳定性，即使线性化系统已被破坏。但通过线性扰动理论证明，当攻击增益略微增加时，能保证广泛非线性系统的内部失稳。

Conclusion: 鲁棒控制理论中的小增益定理不仅可用于设计稳定系统，也可能被恶意利用来构建最小规模的失稳攻击。虽然最小攻击可能不足以破坏非线性系统，但稍微增加攻击增益就能保证广泛非线性系统的内部失稳，这对关键基础设施的安全设计具有重要意义。

Abstract: The robust stability problem involves designing a controlled system which remains stable in the presence of modeling uncertainty. In this context, results known as small gain theorems are used to quantify the maximum amount of uncertainty for which stability is guaranteed. These notions inform the design of numerous control systems, including critical infrastructure components such as power grids, gas pipelines, and water systems. However, these same concepts can be used by an adversary to design a malicious feedback attack, of minimal size, to drive the closed-loop system to instability. In this paper, we first present a detailed review of the results in robust control which allow for the construction of minimal destabilizers. These minimally sized attacks merely push the system to the stability boundary, which we demonstrate do not necessarily destabilize nonlinear systems even when the linearization is destabilized. Our main result leverages linear perturbation theory to explicitly prove, in the state space context, that internal destabilization is guaranteed for a broad class of nonlinear systems when the gain of these attacks is slightly increased.

</details>


### [4] [Transfer Learning in Bayesian Optimization for Aircraft Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28999)
*Ali Tfaily,Youssef Diouane,Nathalie Bartoli,Michael Kokkolaras*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种结合迁移学习和集成代理模型的约束贝叶斯优化方法，用于解决飞机设计中的冷启动问题，通过PLS降维和元数据代理选择处理异构设计变量和约束


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决贝叶斯优化中的冷启动问题，特别是在飞机设计优化中面临的异构设计变量和约束挑战，利用源数据加速目标问题的优化过程

Method: 1) 使用迁移学习的集成代理模型框架；2) 采用偏最小二乘(PLS)降维算法处理设计空间异质性；3) 提出元数据代理选择方法处理约束异质性；4) 在约束贝叶斯优化框架中集成这些方法

Result: 在数值基准问题和飞机概念设计优化问题中，相比标准贝叶斯优化，早期优化迭代收敛显著改善，目标函数和约束代理模型的预测精度均有提升

Conclusion: 所提出的迁移学习约束贝叶斯优化方法能有效解决飞机设计中的冷启动问题，通过处理设计空间和约束的异质性，显著提高了优化效率和预测精度

Abstract: The use of transfer learning within Bayesian optimization addresses the disadvantages of the so-called \textit{cold start} problem by using source data to aid in the optimization of a target problem. We present a method that leverages an ensemble of surrogate models using transfer learning and integrates it in a constrained Bayesian optimization framework. We identify challenges particular to aircraft design optimization related to heterogeneous design variables and constraints. We propose the use of a partial-least-squares dimension reduction algorithm to address design space heterogeneity, and a \textit{meta} data surrogate selection method to address constraint heterogeneity. Numerical benchmark problems and an aircraft conceptual design optimization problem are used to demonstrate the proposed methods. Results show significant improvement in convergence in early optimization iterations compared to standard Bayesian optimization, with improved prediction accuracy for both objective and constraint surrogate models.

</details>


### [5] [Beyond binarity: Semidefinite programming for ternary quadratic problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28979)
*Frank de Meijer,Veronica Piccialli,Renata Sotirov,Antonio M. Sudoso*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对三元二次规划问题(TQP)提出了首个专门的整数半定规划框架，开发了精确求解算法，包括三元SDP公式、理论分析、有效不等式和分支定界策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然对于{0,1}和{±1}值的二次规划问题已有成熟的半定规划技术，但对于变量取值为{0, ±1}的三元二次规划问题，目前缺乏专门的整数半定规划框架。三元二次规划在实践中有多种应用，需要有效的精确求解方法。

Method: 1. 提出了三元SDP公式作为精确求解的基础；2. 推导了秩一三元正半定矩阵的新理论见解；3. 构建了基本的SDP松弛，并通过有效不等式（三角形、RLT、分割和k边形不等式）进行加强；4. 设计了专门的分支定界算法，迭代求解加强的SDP、分离违反的不等式、应用三元分支策略并计算高质量可行解。

Result: 在受实践启发的TQP变体上进行了测试，包括无约束、线性约束和二次比率问题。计算结果表明所提算法在这些实例上具有有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为三元二次规划问题建立了首个整数半定规划框架，通过理论分析、有效不等式和专门的分支定界算法，实现了对TQP的有效精确求解，填补了该领域的研究空白。

Abstract: We study the ternary quadratic problem (TQP), a quadratic optimization problem with linear constraints where the variables take values in $\{0, \pm 1\}$. While semidefinite programming (SDP) techniques are well established for $\{0,1\}$- and $\{\pm 1\}$-valued quadratic problems, no dedicated integer semidefinite programming framework exists for the ternary case. In this paper, we introduce a ternary SDP formulation for the TQP that forms the basis of an exact solution approach. We derive new theoretical insights in rank-one ternary positive semidefinite matrices, which lead to a basic SDP relaxation that is further strengthened by valid triangle, RLT, split and $k$-gonal inequalities. These are embedded in a tailored branch-and-bound algorithm that iteratively solves strengthened SDPs, separates violated inequalities, applies a ternary branching strategy and computes high-quality feasible solutions. We test our algorithm on TQP variations motivated by practice, including unconstrained, linearly constrained and quadratic ratio problems. Computational results on these instances demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed algorithm.

</details>


### [6] [Collisionless Multi-Agent Path Planning in the Hamilton-Jacobi Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28993)
*Christian Parkinson,Adan Baca,Huy Nguyen*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出基于Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman方程的无碰撞多智能体路径规划方法，无需分层规划器，能处理异构智能体和高维动力学系统


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多智能体路径规划方法通常需要分层规划器或黑盒组件，难以处理异构智能体和高维动力学系统。本文旨在开发一种基于最优控制理论和偏微分方程的通用方法，避免这些限制

Method: 基于Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman方程的变分公式开发网格无关数值方法，使用原始-对偶混合梯度优化方案求解，能处理异构智能体和高维动力学问题

Result: 方法在简单汽车和四旋翼无人机路径规划问题上验证有效，能够解析高维问题中的最优轨迹

Conclusion: 基于Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman方程的路径规划方法为多智能体系统提供了一种理论严谨、无需分层规划器的解决方案，特别适用于异构智能体和高维动力学场景

Abstract: We present a method for collisionless multi-agent path planning using the Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equation. Because the method is rooted in optimal control theory and partial differential equations, it avoids the need for hierarchical planners and is black-box free. Our model can account for heterogeneous agents and realistic, high-dimensional dynamics. We develop a grid-free numerical method based on a variational formulation of the solution of the Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equation which can resolve optimal trajectories even in high-dimensional problems, and include some practical implementation notes. In particular, we resolve the solution using a primal-dual hybrid gradient optimization scheme. We demonstrate the method's efficacy on path planning problems involving simple cars and quadcopter drones.

</details>


### [7] [A user-driven pricing and scheduling framework for public electric vehicle charging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29044)
*Fangting Zhou,Jiaming Wu,Balazs Kulcsar*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出用户驱动的电动汽车公共充电定价与调度框架，通过竞价机制协调异构用户需求与有限容量


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运营商定价方案灵活性有限，难以协调异构用户需求与容量约束，导致充电站利用率不均且低效

Method: 三阶段交互框架：用户提交包含时间槽、竞价和数量限制的投标；运营商基于投标确定价格和充电槽分配；用户观察结果后决定是否接受

Result: 数值案例研究揭示了用户接受度、运营商收入和充电容量利用率在不同充电水平下的权衡关系

Conclusion: 该框架为设计灵活定价方案提供实践指导，能更好适应异构用户偏好并提高系统效率

Abstract: Public electric vehicle (EV) charging infrastructure has expanded rapidly, yet utilization across charging stations remains uneven and often inefficient. Existing operator-determined pricing schemes offer limited flexibility to coordinate heterogeneous user demand within constrained capacity. This study proposes a user-driven pricing and scheduling framework for public EV charging. Users submit advance bids specifying acceptable time slots, bid prices, and quantity bounds. Based on these bids, the charging operator determines prices and charging slot assignments. After observing the outcomes, users decide whether to accept the resulting prices and allocations. The operator's decision problem incorporates profit objectives, user participation requirements, and capacity constraints across charging levels and time slots. The framework captures a three-stage interaction involving user bidding, operator decisions, and user acceptance. Numerical case studies reveal trade-offs among user acceptance, operator revenue, and charging capacity utilization under different charging levels. The findings provide practical guidance and insights into designing flexible pricing schemes that better accommodate heterogeneous user preferences while improving system efficiency.

</details>


### [8] [Scalable Co-Design via Linear Design Problems: Compositional Theory and Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29083)
*Yubo Cai,Yujun Huang,Meshal Alharbi,Gioele Zardini*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文提出了线性设计问题(LDPs)作为单调协同设计框架中可精确计算的问题类别，将设计问题转化为多目标线性规划，并开发了计算可行集的两种方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单调协同设计虽然提供了组合语言来处理复杂工程系统的设计问题，但其通用性本身并不能揭示哪些问题类别允许精确且可扩展的计算。需要识别出能够进行精确计算的设计问题类别。

Method: 引入线性设计问题(LDPs)，其可行功能-资源关系是欧几里得偏序集上的多面体。证明LDPs查询可精确转化为多目标线性规划(MOLPs)。开发两种计算可行集的方法：1)保持块角稀疏性的整体提升公式；2)通过多面体投影逐步消除内部变量的组合公式。

Result: LDPs在基本协同设计互连下是封闭的，任何线性组件的互连都会诱导出系统级LDP。凸协同设计资源查询允许任意精度的多面体外近似，对于标准非负资源锥，衰退锥误差为零。数值研究验证了理论。

Conclusion: 线性设计问题为单调协同设计提供了一个可精确计算且可扩展的问题类别，通过多目标线性规划连接了设计语义与多目标优化，为复杂工程系统的设计提供了有效的计算框架。

Abstract: Designing complex engineered systems requires managing tightly coupled trade-offs between subsystem capabilities and resource requirements. Monotone co-design provides a compositional language for such problems, but its generality does not by itself reveal which problem classes admit exact and scalable computation. This paper isolates such a class by introducing Linear Design Problems (LDPs): design problems whose feasible functionality--resource relations are polyhedra over Euclidean posets. We show that queries on LDPs reduce exactly to Multi-Objective Linear Programs (MOLPs), thereby connecting monotone co-design semantics with polyhedral multiobjective optimization. We further prove that LDPs are closed under the fundamental co-design interconnections, implying that any interconnection of linear components induces a system-level LDP. To compute the resulting feasible sets, we develop two complementary constructions: a monolithic lifted formulation that preserves block-angular sparsity, and a compositional formulation that incrementally eliminates internal variables through polyhedral projection. Beyond the exact linear setting, we show that convex co-design resource queries admit arbitrarily accurate polyhedral outer approximations, with recession-cone error identically zero for standard nonnegative resource cones. Numerical studies on synthetic series-chain benchmarks, a gripper, and a rover co-design validate the theory.

</details>


### [9] [Primal-dual dynamics featuring Hessian-driven damping and variable mass for convex optimization problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29124)
*Xiangkai Sun,Feng Guo,Liang He,Xiaole Guo*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种具有变质量和Hessian驱动阻尼的Tikhonov正则化原始-对偶动力系统，用于求解带线性等式约束的凸优化问题，证明了轨迹强收敛到最小范数解，并获得了收敛速率结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决带线性等式约束的凸优化问题，需要设计能够收敛到最小范数解的动力系统。现有方法在收敛速率和参数调整方面存在局限，因此需要开发具有多个时间相关参数（变质量、慢粘性阻尼、外推、时间缩放）的系统，以改善收敛性能。

Method: 提出了一种新的Tikhonov正则化原始-对偶动力系统，包含四个时间相关参数：变质量、慢粘性阻尼、外推项和时间缩放。系统采用Hessian驱动阻尼，通过Lyapunov分析方法研究系统的收敛性质。

Result: 证明了系统轨迹强收敛到优化问题的最小范数解；获得了原始-对偶间隙、目标函数残差和可行性违反的收敛速率；通过参数调整可以改善这些收敛速率；数值实验验证了理论结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的具有变质量和Hessian驱动阻尼的Tikhonov正则化原始-对偶动力系统能够有效求解带线性等式约束的凸优化问题，不仅保证强收敛到最小范数解，而且通过参数调整可以优化收敛性能，为优化算法设计提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: This paper deals with a new Tikhonov regularized primal-dual dynamical system with variable mass and Hessian-driven damping for solving a convex optimization problem with linear equality constraints. The system features several time-dependent parameters: variable mass, slow viscous damping, extrapolation, and temporal scaling. By employing the Lyapunov analysis approach, we obtain the strong convergence of the trajectory generated by the proposed system to the minimal norm solution of the optimization problem, as well as convergence rate results for the primal-dual gap, the objective residual, and the feasibility violation. We also show that the convergence rates of the primal-dual gap, the objective residual, and the feasibility violation can be improved by appropriately adjusting these parameters. Further, we conduct numerical experiments to demonstrate the effectiveness of the theoretical results.

</details>


### [10] [Adaptive Delayed-Update Cyclic Algorithm for Variational Inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29128)
*Yi Wei,Xufeng Cai,Jelena Diakonikolas*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: ADUCA是一种自适应延迟更新的循环算法，用于解决单调Lipschitz算子的Minty变分不等式，无需参数调优或线搜索，具有分布式兼容性和最优复杂度


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环块坐标方法在实践中因其简单性和强经验性能而广泛应用，但其理论行为难以解释，步长设置通常需要仔细调优或线搜索机制。需要开发一种参数自由、无需全局或块级Lipschitz常数、无需每轮线搜索的循环算法

Method: 开发ADUCA算法，采用延迟一个完整周期的算子信息更新策略，这使得算法兼容并行和分布式实现，减少了块间的同步要求。算法在初始化时仅需一次线搜索

Result: ADUCA实现了（接近）最优的全局oracle复杂度：对于单调算子，复杂度按1/ε缩放；对于强单调算子，复杂度按log²(1/ε)缩放

Conclusion: ADUCA为循环块坐标方法提供了理论解释框架，实现了参数自由的自适应算法设计，具有分布式兼容性和最优复杂度保证，解决了传统方法需要调优和线搜索的问题

Abstract: Cyclic block coordinate methods are a fundamental class of first-order algorithms, widely used in practice for their simplicity and strong empirical performance. Yet, their theoretical behavior remains challenging to explain, and setting their step sizes -- beyond classical coordinate descent for minimization -- typically requires careful tuning or line-search machinery. In this work, we develop $\texttt{ADUCA}$ (Adaptive Delayed-Update Cyclic Algorithm), a cyclic algorithm addressing a broad class of Minty variational inequalities with monotone Lipschitz operators. $\texttt{ADUCA}$ is parameter-free: it requires no global or block-wise Lipschitz constants and uses no per-epoch line search, except at initialization. A key feature of the algorithm is using operator information delayed by a full cycle, which makes the algorithm compatible with parallel and distributed implementations, and attractive due to weakened synchronization requirements across blocks. We prove that $\texttt{ADUCA}$ attains (near) optimal global oracle complexity as a function of target error $ε>0,$ scaling with $1/ε$ for monotone operators, or with $\log^2(1/ε)$ for operators that are strongly monotone.

</details>


### [11] [QOCO-GPU: A Quadratic Objective Conic Optimizer with GPU Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29197)
*Govind M. Chari,Behçet Açıkmeşe*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 开发了QOCO求解器的GPU加速后端，基于cuDSS库进行稀疏LDL分解，通过自定义CUDA内核优化锥操作，实现50-70倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有QOCO求解器在处理大规模二次规划和二阶锥规划问题时，CPU实现的计算效率有限，需要利用GPU的并行计算能力来加速求解过程。

Method: 1. 使用NVIDIA cuDSS库对KKT系统进行直接稀疏LDL分解；2. 开发自定义CUDA内核优化锥操作；3. 重构QOCO引入模块化后端抽象，解耦求解逻辑与线性代数实现；4. 提供Python和CVXPY接口。

Result: 在包含数千万到数亿非零元素的KKT矩阵的大规模二次规划和SOCP问题上，GPU后端相比CPU实现获得了50-70倍的加速效果。

Conclusion: GPU加速的QOCO后端显著提升了大规模二次规划和二阶锥规划问题的求解效率，通过模块化设计实现了CPU和GPU后端的代码共享，为大规模优化问题提供了高效的求解方案。

Abstract: We present a GPU-accelerated backend for QOCO, a C-based solver for quadratic objective second-order cone programs (SOCPs) based on a primal-dual interior point method. Our backend uses NVIDIA's cuDSS library to perform a direct sparse LDL factorization of the KKT system at each iteration. We also develop custom CUDA kernels for cone operations and show that parallelizing these operations is essential for achieving peak performance. Additionally, we refactor QOCO to introduce a modular backend abstraction that decouples solver logic from the underlying linear algebra implementations, allowing the existing CPU and new GPU backend to share a unified codebase. This GPU backend is accessible through a direct Python interface and through CVXPY, allowing for easy use. Numerical experiments on a range of large-scale quadratic programs and SOCPs with tens to hundreds of millions of nonzero elements in the KKT matrix, demonstrate speedups of up to 50-70 times over the CPU implementation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在外部量子噪声环境下，如何设计量子记忆系统来保持初始动态变量，通过经典控制信号优化系统性能，解决量子信息存储中的噪声干扰问题。

Result: 1. 将记忆性能泛函与辅助经典控制仿射动力系统的矩阵值状态相关联；2. 提出点对点控制设计方法；3. 在有限时域设置中应用动态规划，获得二次非线性HJB方程，并给出递归计算渐近展开形式的解。

Conclusion: 该研究为量子记忆系统的控制设计提供了系统框架，通过经典控制信号有效抑制量子噪声对记忆性能的影响，点对点控制和动态规划方法为量子信息存储的优化控制提供了理论工具。

Abstract: This paper is concerned with finite-level quantum memory systems for retaining initial dynamic variables in the presence of external quantum noise. The system variables have an algebraic structure, similar to that of the Pauli matrices, and their Heisenberg picture evolution is governed by a quasilinear quantum stochastic differential equation. The latter involves a Hamiltonian whose parameters depend affinely on a classical control signal in the form of a deterministic function of time. The memory performance is quantified by a mean-square deviation of quantum system variables of interest from their initial conditions. We relate this functional to a matrix-valued state of an auxiliary classical control-affine dynamical system. This leads to a pointwise control design where the control signal minimises the time-derivative of the mean-square deviation with an additional quadratic penalty on the control. In an alternative finite-horizon setting with a terminal-integral cost functional, we apply dynamic programming and obtain a quadratically nonlinear Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equation, for which a solution is outlined in the form of a recursively computed asymptotic expansion.

Recent works have proposed systematic constructions of Lyapunov functions for such analysis, while also revealing limitations of the Lyapunov analysis. Aujol--Dossal--Rondepierre (2023) have proposed a technique to address this issue by reorganizing Lyapunov functions so as to evaluate a quantity $f(x(t)) - f_* - g(t)\|x(t)-x_*\|^2$ rather than $f(x(t)) - f_*$. By combining this technique with our computer-assisted framework to discover Lyapunov functions, we develop an improved method that reproduces an existing convergence rate or yields better rates than previous studies.

Abstract: In this paper, a new one-parameter filled function approach is developed for nonlinear multi-objective optimization. Inspired by key filled function ideas from single-objective optimization, the proposed method is adapted to the multi-objective setting. It avoids scalarization weights and does not impose any prior preference ordering among objectives. A descent-based procedure is first applied to obtain a local weak efficient solution. An associated filled function is then constructed and used to derive another local weak efficient solution that improves upon the current one. Numerical experiments on a set of test problems demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach relative to existing methods.

Motivation: 内部人员威胁是团队协作中的严重问题，内部人员表面上合作但暗中追求私人目标，会损害集体绩效、威胁任务成功和操作安全。现有方法通常假设内部人员意图已知，但实际中决策者往往缺乏这种先验知识。

Method: 采用内部人员感知的博弈论框架，将内部人员与决策者的交互建模为连续时间切换系统，每个时间段对应不同的内部人员行为模式或威胁级别。开发周期性离策略缓解方案，使决策者能从在线数据中学习最优缓解策略，无需内部人员意图的先验知识。通过设计适当的学习间隔时间条件，确保学习过程和闭环系统的收敛性。

Result: 建立了学习过程和闭环系统的收敛性保证，并表征了决策者实现的相应缓解性能。该方案能够在决策者缺乏内部人员意图先验知识的情况下，有效应对不同类型的内部人员威胁。

Conclusion: 提出的周期性离策略缓解方案为处理内部人员威胁提供了有效的理论框架，使决策者能够在未知内部人员意图的情况下在线学习最优缓解策略，并通过理论分析确保了系统的收敛性和性能保证。

Abstract: An insider is a team member who covertly deviates from the team's optimal collaborative strategy to pursue a private objective while still appearing cooperative. Such an insider may initially behave cooperatively but later switch to selfish or malicious actions, thereby degrading collective performance, threatening mission success, and compromising operational safety. In this paper, we study such insider threats within an insider-aware, game-theoretic formulation, where the insider interacts with a decision maker (DM) under a continuous-time switched system, with each time interval characterized by a distinct insider behavioral pattern or threat level. We develop a periodic off-policy mitigation scheme that enables the DM to learn optimal mitigation policies from online data when encountering different insider threats, without requiring a priori knowledge of insider intentions. By designing appropriate conditions on the inter-learning interval time, we establish convergence guarantees for both the learning process and the closed-loop system, and characterize the corresponding mitigation performance achieved by the DM.

</details>


### [21] [Quantitative Uniqueness of Kantorovich Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29595)
*William Ford*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 研究对偶最优输运问题解的唯一性，包括定性唯一性（解在常数意义下唯一）和定量唯一性（最优解集直径的界）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统最优输运理论中，对偶问题的解（对偶势）通常只在可微性假设下具有唯一性。本文旨在建立更一般的唯一性理论，适用于边缘测度支撑在低维子集或对偶势无处可微的情况。

Method: 1. 定性分析：证明当一边缘测度的支撑是"可求长连通"（通过可求长路径连通）时，最优对偶势在常数意义下唯一。2. 定量分析：通过将最优对偶势集合表征为显式半空间族的交集，用一边缘测度支撑与正则连通集的Hausdorff距离来控制最优解集的直径。

Result: 1. 建立了首个适用于边缘测度支撑在低维子集情况下的唯一性结果。2. 证明了对偶势即使无处可微，在可求长连通条件下仍具有唯一性。3. 提供了最优解集直径的定量界，量化了"几乎连通"支撑下解的"几乎唯一性"。

Conclusion: 本文发展了对偶最优输运问题解的唯一性理论，突破了传统可微性假设的限制，为边缘测度支撑在低维子集或对偶势无处可微的情况提供了首个一般性唯一性结果，并建立了定量控制框架。

Abstract: This paper studies the uniqueness of solutions to the dual optimal transport problem, both qualitatively and quantitatively (bounds on the diameter of the set of optimisers).
  On the qualitative side, we prove that when one marginal measure's support is rectifiably connected (path-connected by rectifiable paths), the optimal dual potentials are unique up to a constant. This represents the first uniqueness result applicable even when both marginal measures are concentrated on lower-dimensional subsets of the ambient space, and also applies in cases where optimal potentials are nowhere differentiable on the supports of the marginals.
  On the quantitative side, we control the diameter of the set of optimal dual potentials by the Hausdorff distance between the support of one of the marginal measures and a regular connected set. In this way, we quantify the extent to which optimisers are almost unique when the support of one marginal measure is almost connected. This is a consequence of a novel characterisation of the set of optimal dual potentials as the intersection of an explicit family of half-spaces.

</details>


### [22] [An objective-function-free algorithm for nonconvex stochastic optimization with deterministic equality and inequality constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29685)
*S. Gratton,Ph. L. Toint*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种用于求解具有随机目标和确定性约束的优化问题的算法，该算法仅使用目标函数的梯度而不评估函数值，基于自适应选择函数递减和约束改进迭代，在满秩雅可比矩阵条件下达到O(1/√k)收敛率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决具有随机目标函数和确定性约束的优化问题，传统方法需要评估目标函数值，但某些应用中函数值难以计算或成本高昂。需要开发仅使用梯度信息而不依赖函数值评估的高效算法。

Method: 提出一种目标函数无关的算法，仅使用目标函数的梯度信息。算法基于自适应选择两种迭代：函数递减迭代（使用Adagrad型步长）和约束改进迭代。通过动态平衡这两种迭代来同时处理目标优化和约束满足。

Result: 当应用于具有满秩雅可比矩阵的问题时，证明联合原始-对偶最优性度量以O(1/√k)的速率下降，这与无约束情况下一阶方法的收敛率相同。算法在仅使用梯度信息的情况下实现了与完整函数评估方法相当的收敛性能。

Conclusion: 该算法成功解决了仅使用梯度信息的随机约束优化问题，在满秩条件下实现了最优收敛率。方法为那些目标函数值难以评估但梯度可得的实际问题提供了有效的解决方案，扩展了一阶方法在约束优化中的应用范围。

Abstract: An algorithm is proposed for solving optimization problems with stochastic objective and deterministic equality and inequality constraints. This algorithm is objective-function-free in the sense that it only uses the objective's gradient and never evaluates the function value. It is based on an adaptive selection of function-decreasing and constraint-improving iterations, the first ones using an Adagrad-type stepsize. When applied to problems with full-rank Jacobian, the combined primal-dual optimality measure is shown to decrease at the rate of O(1/sqrt{k}), which is identical to the convergence rate of first-order methods in the unconstrained case.

</details>

*Amos Uderzo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In the present paper, a systematic study is made of quantitative semicontinuity (a.k.a. Lipschitzian) properties of certain multifunctions, which are defined as a solution map associated to a family of parameterized ``split" feasibility problems. The latter are a particular class of convex feasibility problems with well recognized applications to several areas of engineering and systems biology. As a part of a perturbation analysis of variational systems, this study falls within the framework of a line of research pursued by several authors. It is performed by means of techniques of variational analysis, which lead to establish sufficient conditions for the Lipschitz lower semicontinuity, calmness, isolated calmness, Lipschitz upper semicontinuity and Aubin property of the solution map. Along with each of these properties, a quantitative estimate of the related exact bound is also provided. The key elements emerging on the way to achieving the main results are dual regularity conditions qualifying the problem behaviour, which are expressed in terms of convex analysis constructions involving problem data. The approach here proposed tries to unify the study of the aforementioned properties.

Abstract: This paper addresses the problem of steering a state distribution over a finite horizon in discrete time with output feedback. In particular, this paper extends existing distribution steering formulations to scenarios in which estimation errors are not orthogonal to the state estimates. A general framework is developed to capture this non-orthogonality, and the resulting problem is formulated in a form solvable via sequential convex programming with rank constraints. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多控制器系统中，当存在延迟和非对称信息结构时，经典的分离原理失效，估计与控制设计强耦合，难以推导显式纳什均衡。

Method: 采用公共-私有信息分解方法，解耦控制输入和状态估计；应用前向迭代法建立耦合的Riccati方程和估计误差协方差递推的收敛性。

Result: 获得了稳态卡尔曼滤波器和纳什均衡的闭式解；量化了非对称信息的影响，证明信息更丰富的玩家成本更低；数值算例验证了结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的信息分解方法成功解决了延迟和非对称信息结构下的多控制器博弈问题，为这类复杂信息结构下的控制设计提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We address a noncooperative game problem in multi-controller system under delayed and asymmetric information structure. Under these conditions, the classical separation principle fails as estimation and control design become strongly coupled, complicating the derivation of an explicit Nash equilibrium. To resolve this, we employ a common-private information decomposition approach, effectively decoupling control inputs and state estimation to obtain a closed-form Nash equilibrium. By applying a forward iterative method, we establish the convergence of the coupled Riccati and estimation error covariance recursions, yielding both the steady-state Kalman filter and the Nash equilibrium. Furthermore, we quantify the impact of asymmetric information, proving that a richer information set reduces the costs for the corresponding player. Finally, numerical examples are provided to demonstrate the effectiveness of the results.

### [26] [Analyzing Performance and Scalability of Benders Decomposition for Generation and Transmission Expansion Planning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29867)
*David L. Cole,Michael Lau,Xinliang Dai,Sambuddha Chakrabarti,Jesse D. Jenkins*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了在具有节点分辨率和DCOPF约束的GTEP模型中改进Benders分解性能的策略，包括GBD、热启动、主问题线性松弛和正则化等方法，成功解决了原本难以处理的大规模混合整数规划问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GTEP问题能够提供比传统发电或输电扩展规划更好的决策，但计算复杂度高或难以处理。Benders分解已应用于扩展规划问题，但需要加速收敛策略来提高性能。

Method: 测试了多种加速Benders分解的策略组合：广义Benders分解（GBD）、通过传输约束模型热启动、使用主问题的线性松弛、以及正则化技术。还提出了处理双线性约束的替代方法。在包含146个节点（1000万连续变量和400个混合整数决策）的MILP GTEP模型上进行测试。

Result: 采用加速Benders分解方法后，原本难以处理的问题可以在5小时内求解到1%的间隙。结果表明，在初始热启动和松弛步骤中使用正则化，完成后关闭正则化，通常是策略的最佳组合。

Conclusion: 通过精心设计的加速Benders分解策略组合，可以有效解决大规模GTEP问题，其中在初始阶段使用正则化并在后续关闭的策略表现最佳，为解决计算复杂的扩展规划问题提供了有效方法。

Abstract: Generation and Transmission Expansion Planning (GTEP) problems co-optimize generation and transmission expansion, enabling them to provide better planning decisions than traditional Generation Expansion Planning or Transmission Expansion Planning problems, but GTEPs can be computationally complex or intractable. Benders Decomposition (BD) has been applied to expansion planning problems, with various methods applied to accelerate convergence. In this work, we test strategies for improving the performance of BD on GTEP models with nodal resolution and DCOPF constraints. We also present an alternative approach for handling the bilinear constraints that can result in these problems. These tests included combinations of using generalized Benders decomposition (GBD), hot-starting via a transport constrained model, using linear relaxations of the master problem, and using regularization. We test these methods on mixed-integer linear programming GTEP models with up to 146 buses (10 million continuous variables and 400 mixed-integer decisions). With selected accelerated Benders decomposition approaches, the problems can be solved to under a 1\% gap in as little as 5 hours where they were otherwise intractable. Results also suggest that using regularization on these initial hot-starting and relaxation steps and turning it off after they are complete was generally the best combination of strategies.

### [29] [ChartDiff: A Large-Scale Benchmark for Comprehending Pairs of Charts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28902)
*Rongtian Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ChartDiff是首个大规模跨图表比较摘要基准，包含8,541个图表对，用于评估模型在跨图表比较推理方面的能力，揭示了词汇重叠与实际摘要质量之间的不匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图表理解基准主要关注单图表解释，缺乏对跨图表比较推理的评估。为了填补这一空白，需要创建专门针对跨图表比较摘要的基准数据集。

Method: 构建ChartDiff基准，包含8,541个图表对，涵盖多样数据源、图表类型和视觉风格。每个图表对都有LLM生成并经人工验证的摘要，描述趋势、波动和异常差异。使用该基准评估通用模型、图表专用模型和基于流水线的模型。

Result: 前沿通用模型在GPT-based质量评估中表现最佳，而专用和流水线方法在ROUGE得分上更高但人类对齐评估较低，显示词汇重叠与实际摘要质量不匹配。多序列图表对所有模型家族都具有挑战性，而强大的端到端模型对绘图库差异相对稳健。

Conclusion: 比较性图表推理对当前视觉语言模型仍是重大挑战，ChartDiff为推进多图表理解研究提供了新基准。

Abstract: Charts are central to analytical reasoning, yet existing benchmarks for chart understanding focus almost exclusively on single-chart interpretation rather than comparative reasoning across multiple charts. To address this gap, we introduce ChartDiff, the first large-scale benchmark for cross-chart comparative summarization. ChartDiff consists of 8,541 chart pairs spanning diverse data sources, chart types, and visual styles, each annotated with LLM-generated and human-verified summaries describing differences in trends, fluctuations, and anomalies. Using ChartDiff, we evaluate general-purpose, chart-specialized, and pipeline-based models. Our results show that frontier general-purpose models achieve the highest GPT-based quality, while specialized and pipeline-based methods obtain higher ROUGE scores but lower human-aligned evaluation, revealing a clear mismatch between lexical overlap and actual summary quality. We further find that multi-series charts remain challenging across model families, whereas strong end-to-end models are relatively robust to differences in plotting libraries. Overall, our findings demonstrate that comparative chart reasoning remains a significant challenge for current vision-language models and position ChartDiff as a new benchmark for advancing research on multi-chart understanding.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AGI研究缺乏形式化定义和理论框架，各大科技公司投入巨大资源但缺乏系统性的理论指导。需要建立数学严谨的框架来统一描述不同AGI架构，明确其共性与差异，指导未来研究方向。

Method: 采用范畴论作为形式化工具，借鉴"范畴中的机器"概念，构建AGI架构的范畴论框架。具体包括：1) 将RL、因果RL、基于图式的学习等架构形式化为范畴中的对象；2) 定义架构间的态射关系；3) 建立统一的形式基础，整合架构结构、信息组织、智能体实现、环境交互、行为发展和实证评估。

Result: 初步实现了强化学习、因果强化学习和基于图式学习架构的范畴论形式化，为比较不同AGI架构提供了数学基础。建立了支持定义架构属性（句法、信息、语义）和智能体评估的框架。

Conclusion: 范畴论与AGI将形成共生关系，该框架为AGI研究提供了统一的形式化基础，能够明确不同架构的共性与差异，揭示未来研究方向，支持AGI系统的理论发展和实证评估。

Abstract: AGI has become the Holly Grail of AI with the promise of level intelligence and the major Tech companies around the world are investing unprecedented amounts of resources in its pursuit. Yet, there does not exist a single formal definition and only some empirical AGI benchmarking frameworks currently exist. The main purpose of this paper is to develop a general, algebraic and category theoretic framework for describing, comparing and analysing different possible AGI architectures. Thus, this Category theoretic formalization would also allow to compare different possible candidate AGI architectures, such as, RL, Universal AI, Active Inference, CRL, Schema based Learning, etc. It will allow to unambiguously expose their commonalities and differences, and what is even more important, expose areas for future research. From the applied Category theoretic point of view, we take as inspiration Machines in a Category to provide a modern view of AGI Architectures in a Category. More specifically, this first position paper provides, on one hand, a first exercise on RL, Causal RL and SBL Architectures in a Category, and on the other hand, it is a first step on a broader research program that seeks to provide a unified formal foundation for AGI systems, integrating architectural structure, informational organization, agent realization, agent and environment interaction, behavioural development over time, and the empirical evaluation of properties. This framework is also intended to support the definition of architectural properties, both syntactic and informational, as well as semantic properties of agents and their assessment in environments with explicitly characterized features. We claim that Category Theory and AGI will have a very symbiotic relation.

Abstract: This paper presents the World-Action Model (WAM), an action-regularized world model that jointly reasons over future visual observations and the actions that drive state transitions. We evaluate WAM on enhancing policy learning across eight manipulation tasks from the CALVIN benchmark. We first pretrain a diffusion policy via behavioral cloning on world model latents, then refine it with model-based PPO inside the frozen world model. Our results further reveal that models respond heterogeneously to multi-agent decomposition and iterative learning, indicating that the benefits of workflow evolution depend on the capabilities of the underlying execution model. Beyond these benchmarks, Mimosa modular architecture and tool-agnostic design make it readily extensible, and its fully logged execution traces and archived workflows support auditability by preserving every analytical step for inspection and potential replication. Combined with domain-expert guidance, the framework has the potential to automate a broad range of computationally accessible scientific tasks across disciplines. Released as a fully open-source platform, Mimosa aims to provide an open foundation for community-driven ASR.

Result: 自主行为在当前LLM智能体中已经涌现：智能体自发发明专门角色、自愿放弃能力范围外的任务、形成浅层层级结构。混合协议比集中协调性能提升14%，协议间质量差异达44%。涌现的自主程度随模型能力提升而增强，系统可扩展至256个智能体而无质量下降，从8个智能体产生了5,006个独特角色。

Abstract: How much autonomy can multi-agent LLM systems sustain -- and what enables it? We present a 25,000-task computational experiment spanning 8 models, 4--256 agents, and 8 coordination protocols ranging from externally imposed hierarchy to emergent self-organization. We observe that autonomous behavior already emerges in current LLM agents: given minimal structural scaffolding (fixed ordering), agents spontaneously invent specialized roles, voluntarily abstain from tasks outside their competence, and form shallow hierarchies -- without any pre-assigned roles or external design. A hybrid protocol (Sequential) that enables this autonomy outperforms centralized coordination by 14% (p<0.001), with a 44% quality spread between protocols (Cohen's d=1.86, p<0.0001). The degree of emergent autonomy scales with model capability: strong models self-organize effectively, while models below a capability threshold still benefit from rigid structure -- suggesting that as foundation models improve, the scope for autonomous coordination will expand. The system scales sub-linearly to 256 agents without quality degradation (p=0.61), producing 5,006 unique roles from just 8 agents. Results replicate across closed- and open-source models, with open-source achieving 95% of closed-source quality at 24x lower cost. The practical implication: give agents a mission, a protocol, and a capable model -- not a pre-assigned role.

Abstract: The way we're thinking about generative AI right now is fundamentally individual. We argue that we should abandon this approach if we're hoping for AI to support groundbreaking innovation and scientific discovery. Drawing on research and formal results in complex systems, organizational behavior, and philosophy of science, we show why we should expect deep intellectual breakthroughs to come from epistemically diverse groups of AI agents working together rather than singular superintelligent agents. Having a diverse team broadens the search for solutions, delays premature consensus, and allows for the pursuit of unconventional approaches. Developing diverse AI teams also addresses AI critics' concerns that current models are constrained by past data and lack the creative insight required for innovation. The upshot, we argue, is that the future of transformative transformer-based AI is fundamentally many, not one.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在多跳问答中存在局限性：迭代检索系统可能因早期锁定低召回轨迹而放大下游错误，而纯规划方法生成的静态查询集无法适应中间证据变化

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) remain brittle on multi-hop question answering (MHQA), where answering requires combining evidence across documents through retrieval and reasoning. Iterative retrieval systems can fail by locking onto an early low-recall trajectory and amplifying downstream errors, while planning-only approaches may produce static query sets that cannot adapt when intermediate evidence changes. We propose \textbf{Planned Active Retrieval and Reasoning RAG (PAR$^2$-RAG)}, a two-stage framework that separates \emph{coverage} from \emph{commitment}. PAR$^2$-RAG first performs breadth-first anchoring to build a high-recall evidence frontier, then applies depth-first refinement with evidence sufficiency control in an iterative loop. Across four MHQA benchmarks, PAR$^2$-RAG consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art baselines, compared with IRCoT, PAR$^2$-RAG achieves up to \textbf{23.5\%} higher accuracy, with retrieval gains of up to \textbf{10.5\%} in NDCG.

We release a synthetic dataset constructed on real user interactions on a global short-form video platform. Our dataset contains both implicit and explicit engagement signals and rich textual descriptions. Our findings reveal performance bottlenecks in current LLMs, particularly their limited ability to accurately count and attribute engagement signals across heterogeneous interaction types.

TL;DR: SciVisAgentBench是一个用于评估科学数据分析和可视化智能体的综合性基准测试，包含108个专家设计的测试案例，采用多模态评估管道，旨在推动科学可视化智能体的系统化发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的智能体系统能够将自然语言意图转换为可执行的科学可视化任务，但社区缺乏一个原则性、可复现的基准来在真实多步骤分析场景中评估这些新兴的科学可视化智能体。

Method: 提出了SciVisAgentBench基准，基于四维结构化分类法（应用领域、数据类型、复杂度级别、可视化操作），包含108个专家设计的测试案例。开发了多模态结果中心评估管道，结合基于LLM的评判和确定性评估器（图像指标、代码检查器、规则验证器、案例特定评估器）。进行了有效性研究，比较人类专家与LLM评判者的一致性。

Result: 评估了代表性科学可视化智能体和通用编码智能体，建立了初始基线并揭示了能力差距。有效性研究表明人类与LLM评判者之间具有良好一致性。基准测试作为"活基准"支持系统化比较、诊断失败模式并推动科学可视化智能体发展。

Conclusion: SciVisAgentBench提供了一个全面、可扩展的基准测试框架，用于评估科学数据分析和可视化智能体，填补了该领域缺乏原则性评估标准的空白，旨在促进科学可视化智能体技术的系统化进步。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have enabled agentic systems that translate natural language intent into executable scientific visualization (SciVis) tasks. Despite rapid progress, the community lacks a principled and reproducible benchmark for evaluating these emerging SciVis agents in realistic, multi-step analysis settings. We present SciVisAgentBench, a comprehensive and extensible benchmark for evaluating scientific data analysis and visualization agents. Our benchmark is grounded in a structured taxonomy spanning four dimensions: application domain, data type, complexity level, and visualization operation. It currently comprises 108 expert-crafted cases covering diverse SciVis scenarios. To enable reliable assessment, we introduce a multimodal outcome-centric evaluation pipeline that combines LLM-based judging with deterministic evaluators, including image-based metrics, code checkers, rule-based verifiers, and case-specific evaluators. We also conduct a validity study with 12 SciVis experts to examine the agreement between human and LLM judges. Using this framework, we evaluate representative SciVis agents and general-purpose coding agents to establish initial baselines and reveal capability gaps. SciVisAgentBench is designed as a living benchmark to support systematic comparison, diagnose failure modes, and drive progress in agentic SciVis. The benchmark is available at https://scivisagentbench.github.io/.

Method: REFINE采用多智能体架构：1)基于教学原理的反馈生成智能体；2)使用LLM-as-a-judge引导的再生循环，采用人类对齐的法官模型；3)支持学生后续问题的自反思工具调用交互智能体，提供上下文感知、可操作的响应。系统可在本地部署，基于小型开源语言模型。

Abstract: Formative feedback is central to effective learning, yet providing timely, individualised feedback at scale remains a persistent challenge. In this work, we introduce REFINE, a locally deployable, multi-agent feedback system built on small, open-source LLMs that treats feedback as an interactive process. REFINE combines a pedagogically-grounded feedback generation agent with an LLM-as-a-judge-guided regeneration loop using a human-aligned judge, and a self-reflective tool-calling interactive agent that supports student follow-up questions with context-aware, actionable responses. We evaluate REFINE through controlled experiments and an authentic classroom deployment in an undergraduate computer science course. Automatic evaluations show that judge-guided regeneration significantly improves feedback quality, and that the interactive agent produces efficient, high-quality responses comparable to a state-of-the-art closed-source model. Analysis of real student interactions further reveals distinct engagement patterns and indicates that system-generated feedback systematically steers subsequent student inquiry. Our findings demonstrate the feasibility and effectiveness of multi-agent, tool-augmented feedback systems for scalable, interactive feedback.

### [45] [Route-Induced Density and Stability (RIDE): Controlled Intervention and Mechanism Analysis of Routing-Style Meta Prompts on LLM Internal States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29206)
*Dianxing Zhang,Gang Li,Sheng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过注入路由式元提示作为文本代理，测试了稀疏性-确定性假说，发现元提示反而使早期/中间层表示更密集而非稀疏，自然语言专家指令通常优于结构化标签，且密度化与稳定性关联微弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试路由中普遍存在的"稀疏性-确定性假说"——即路由到任务"专家"会激活更稀疏的内部计算，从而产生更确定和稳定的输出。研究者希望验证这一假设是否成立。

Method: 使用路由式元提示作为文本代理，注入到冻结的指令调优LLMs前。通过三个指标量化：(1)激活稀疏性衡量内部密度，(2)领域关键词注意力，(3)通过预测熵和语义变化衡量输出稳定性。在RouterEval子集上测试了三个指令调优模型。

Result: 元提示一致地使早期/中间层表示更密集而非增加稀疏性；自然语言专家指令通常强于结构化标签。注意力响应异质：Qwen/Llama减少关键词注意力，而Mistral增强它。密度化-稳定性关联微弱，仅在Qwen中出现，Llama和Mistral中相关性接近零。

Conclusion: 研究提出了RIDE作为诊断探针，用于校准路由设计和不确定性估计。结果表明稀疏性-确定性假说在测试条件下不成立，为路由机制的理解和优化提供了实证基础。

Abstract: Routing is widely used to scale large language models, from Mixture-of-Experts gating to multi-model/tool selection. A common belief is that routing to a task ``expert'' activates sparser internal computation and thus yields more certain and stable outputs (the Sparsity--Certainty Hypothesis). We test this belief by injecting routing-style meta prompts as a textual proxy for routing signals in front of frozen instruction-tuned LLMs. We quantify (C1) internal density via activation sparsity, (C2) domain-keyword attention, and (C3) output stability via predictive entropy and semantic variation. On a RouterEval subset with three instruction-tuned models (Qwen3-8B, Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, and Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.2), meta prompts consistently densify early/middle-layer representations rather than increasing sparsity; natural-language expert instructions are often stronger than structured tags. Attention responses are heterogeneous: Qwen/Llama reduce keyword attention, while Mistral reinforces it. Finally, the densification--stability link is weak and appears only in Qwen, with near-zero correlations in Llama and Mistral. We present RIDE as a diagnostic probe for calibrating routing design and uncertainty estimation.

</details>


### [46] [Xuanwu: Evolving General Multimodal Models into an Industrial-Grade Foundation for Content Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29211)
*Zhiqian Zhang,Xu Zhao,Xiaoqing Xu,Guangdong Liang,Weijia Wang,Xiaolei Lv,Bo Li,Jun Gao*

Method: 采用紧凑的InternViT-300M + MLP + Qwen3 1.7B架构，在约2B参数预算内平衡细粒度视觉感知、语言语义对齐和部署成本。开发数据迭代和筛选机制，通过渐进式三阶段训练流程：预训练、中间训练和后训练。

Result: 在七个OpenCompass多模态指标上平均得分67.90（优于InternVL 3.5 2B的64.27）；在七个独立业务审核任务中平均召回率94.38%；在具有挑战性的对抗性OCR场景中，对违规文本的加权总体召回率达到82.82%，优于Gemini-2.5-Pro（76.72%）。

Conclusion: 在有限参数预算下，Xuanwu VL-2B实现了业务对齐、视觉感知、通用能力保留和部署成本之间的实用平衡，展示了通用多模态模型向工业级基础模型转化的可行性。

Abstract: In recent years, multimodal large models have continued to improve on general benchmarks. However, in real-world content moderation and adversarial settings, mainstream models still suffer from degraded generalization and catastrophic forgetting because of limited fine-grained visual perception and insufficient modeling of long-tail noise. In this paper, we present Xuanwu VL-2B as a case study of how general multimodal models can be developed into an industrial-grade foundation model for content ecosystems. The model adopts a compact InternViT-300M + MLP + Qwen3 1.7B architecture, balancing fine-grained visual perception, language-semantic alignment, and deployment cost within an approximately 2B-parameter budget. To balance business specialization with the retention of general capabilities, we developed a data iteration and curation mechanism and trained the model through a progressive three-stage pipeline: pre-training, mid-training, and post-training. Ablation studies and offline business evaluations show that Xuanwu VL-2B achieves an average score of 67.90 across seven OpenCompass multimodal metrics (vs. 64.27 for InternVL 3.5 2B), an average recall of 94.38% over seven independent business moderation tasks, and a weighted overall recall of 82.82% on policy-violating text in challenging adversarial OCR scenarios, outperforming Gemini-2.5-Pro (76.72%). These results show that, under a limited parameter budget, Xuanwu VL-2B achieves a practical balance among business alignment, visual perception, general capability retention, and deployment cost.

### [47] [Beyond pass@1: A Reliability Science Framework for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29231)
*Aaditya Khanal,Yangyang Tao,Junxiu Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出可靠性科学框架，评估LLM智能体在长时程任务中的表现，发现能力与可靠性在长时程任务中系统性分离，传统单次成功率指标无法捕捉这种差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要衡量模型在单次尝试中的能力，但生产部署需要可靠性——在重复尝试和不同时长任务中保持一致的性能。研究发现随着任务时长增加，能力与可靠性会系统性分离，而传统pass@1指标对此视而不见。

Method: 引入可靠性科学框架，包含四个指标：可靠性衰减曲线(RDC)、方差放大因子(VAF)、优雅退化分数(GDS)和崩溃起始点(MOP)。在包含396个任务的基准上评估10个模型，涵盖4个时长段和3个领域，共23,392个任务片段。

Result: 关键发现：(1)可靠性衰减具有领域分层性——软件工程GDS从0.90降至0.44，文档处理几乎持平(0.74到0.71)；(2)VAF按能力层级分叉——高VAF是能力特征而非不稳定信号；(3)能力与可靠性排名显著分离，长时程任务中出现多级排名反转；(4)前沿模型崩溃率最高(达19%)，因其尝试雄心勃勃的多步策略有时会失控；(5)记忆支架在所有10个模型中普遍损害长时程性能。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明可靠性应与能力并列作为首要评估维度，传统单次成功率指标不足以评估生产环境中的实际表现，特别是在长时程任务中。

Abstract: Existing benchmarks measure capability -- whether a model succeeds on a single attempt -- but production deployments
  require reliability -- consistent success across repeated attempts on tasks of varying duration. We show these
  properties diverge systematically as task duration grows, and that pass@1 on short tasks is structurally blind to
  this divergence.
  We introduce a reliability science framework for long-horizon LLM agents with four metrics: Reliability Decay Curve
  (RDC), Variance Amplification Factor (VAF), Graceful Degradation Score (GDS), and Meltdown Onset Point (MOP). We
  evaluate 10 models across 23,392 episodes on a 396-task benchmark spanning four duration buckets and three domains.
  Key findings: (1) reliability decay is domain-stratified -- SE GDS drops from 0.90 to 0.44 while document processing
  is nearly flat (0.74 to 0.71); (2) VAF bifurcates by capability tier -- high VAF is a capability signature, not an
  instability signal; (3) capability and reliability rankings diverge substantially, with multi-rank inversions at long
  horizons; (4) frontier models have the highest meltdown rates (up to 19%) because they attempt ambitious multi-step
  strategies that sometimes spiral; and (5) memory scaffolds universally hurt long-horizon performance across all 10
  models. These results motivate reliability as a first-class evaluation dimension alongside capability.

</details>

We propose that grokking originates from a spontaneous simplification of internal model structures governed by the principle of parsimony. Existing GUI agent benchmarks cannot adequately capture this personalization dimension due to sparse user-specific data and the lack of fine-grained evaluation metrics. To address this gap, we present PSPA-Bench, the benchmark dedicated to evaluating personalization in smartphone GUI agents. PSPA-Bench comprises over 12,855 personalized instructions aligned with real-world user behaviors across 10 representative daily-use scenarios and 22 mobile apps, and introduces a structure-aware process evaluation method that measures agents' personalized capabilities at a fine-grained level. Through PSPA-Bench, we benchmark 11 state-of-the-art GUI agents. Results reveal that current methods perform poorly under personalized settings, with even the strongest agent achieving limited success. Our analysis further highlights three directions for advancing personalized GUI agents: (1) reasoning-oriented models consistently outperform general LLMs, (2) perception remains a simple yet critical capability, and (3) reflection and long-term memory mechanisms are key to improving adaptation. Abstract: We introduce Nomad, a system for autonomous data exploration and insight discovery. As a result, query-driven question answering and prompt-driven deep-research systems remain limited by human framing and often fail to cover the broader insight space.

It generates and selects hypotheses and investigates them with an explorer agent that can use document search, web search, and database tools. Candidate insights are then checked by an independent verifier before entering a reporting pipeline that produces cited reports and higher-level meta-reports.
  We also present a comprehensive evaluation framework for autonomous discovery systems that measures trustworthiness, report quality, and diversity. Using a corpus of selected UN and WHO reports, we show that \nomad{} produces more trustworthy and higher-quality reports than baselines, while also producing more diverse insights over several runs.
  Nomad is a step toward autonomous systems that not only answer user questions or conduct directed research, but also discover which questions, research directions, and insights are worth surfacing in the first place.

Method: 引入有效维度(ED)作为基准分数谱的参与比，应用于22个基准测试、8个领域、超过8400个模型评估，通过零假设、可靠性和饱和分析进行补充验证

Applied at per-instance granularity to 22 benchmarks across 8 domains and more than 8,400 model evaluations, ED reveals substantial redundancy: the six-score Open LLM Leaderboard behaves like roughly two effective measurement axes (ED = 1.7), BBH and MMLU-Pro are near-interchangeable (rho = 0.96, stable across seven subpopulations), and measurement breadth varies more than 20x across current benchmarks. We show that relative ED rankings are stable under matched-dimension controls and that ED can flag redundant suite components, monitor performance-conditional compression, and guide benchmark maintenance. Because binary spectra overestimate absolute latent dimensionality, we interpret ED as a screening statistic rather than a literal factor count and complement it with null, reliability, and saturation analyses. We provide a 22-benchmark reference atlas and a four-step diagnostic workflow that benchmark maintainers can run with a score matrix and a few lines of code.

### [55] [Structural Compactness as a Complementary Criterion for Explanation Quality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29491)
*Mohammad Mahdi Mesgari,Jackie Ma,Wojciech Samek,Sebastian Lapuschkin,Leander Weber*

Abstract: In the evaluation of attribution quality, the quantitative assessment of explanation legibility is particularly difficult, as it is influenced by varying shapes and internal organization of attributions not captured by simple statistics. These components are combined into a single score that evaluates compactness, favoring attributions with salient points spread across a small area and spatially organized into few but cohesive clusters. We show that MST-C reliably distinguishes between explanation methods, exposes fundamental structural differences between models, and provides a robust, self-contained diagnostic for explanation compactness that complements existing notions of attribution complexity.

### [56] [Metriplector: From Field Theory to Neural Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29496)
*Dan Oprisa,Peter Toth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Metriplector是一种神经架构原语，将输入配置为抽象物理系统（场、源、算子），系统动力学即为计算过程。通过耦合度量-泊松动力学演化多个场，利用诺特定理导出的应力-能量张量作为输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出一种基于物理系统动力学的神经计算框架，将机器学习任务建模为物理系统的演化过程，利用度量-泊松结构统一处理可逆和耗散动力学，实现从简单到复杂任务的统一处理。

Method: 输入配置抽象物理系统（场、源、算子），多个场通过耦合度量-泊松动力学演化。使用诺特定理导出的应力-能量张量T^{μν}作为输出。该框架支持从纯耗散分支（求解屏蔽泊松方程）到完整度量-泊松结构（包含反对称泊松括号）的频谱实现。

Result: 在四个领域评估：1）迷宫路径规划：15×15网格训练，39×39网格测试，F1=1.0；2）数独求解：零结构注入，97.2%精确求解率；3）CIFAR-100：81.03%准确率，226万参数；4）语言建模：1.182 bits/byte，比GPT基线少3.6倍训练token。

Conclusion: Metriplector作为一种基于物理系统动力学的神经架构原语，能够统一处理从简单约束满足到复杂感知和语言建模的多种任务，展示了物理启发的计算框架在机器学习中的潜力。

Abstract: We present Metriplector, a neural architecture primitive in which the input configures an abstract physical system--fields, sources, and operators--and the dynamics of that system is the computation. Multiple fields evolve via coupled metriplectic dynamics, and the stress-energy tensor T^{μν}, derived from Noether's theorem, provides the readout. The metriplectic formulation admits a natural spectrum of instantiations: the dissipative branch alone yields a screened Poisson equation solved exactly via conjugate gradient; activating the full structure--including the antisymmetric Poisson bracket--gives field dynamics for image recognition and language modeling. We evaluate Metriplector across four domains, each using a task-specific architecture built from this shared primitive with progressively richer physics: F1=1.0 on maze pathfinding, generalizing from 15x15 training grids to unseen 39x39 grids; 97.2% exact Sudoku solve rate with zero structural injection; 81.03% on CIFAR-100 with 2.26M parameters; and 1.182 bits/byte on language modeling with 3.6x fewer training tokens than a GPT baseline.

### [57] [Learning to Generate Formally Verifiable Step-by-Step Logic Reasoning via Structured Formal Intermediaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29500)
*Luoxin Chen,Yichi Zhou,Huishuai Zhang*

TL;DR: PRoSFI是一种通过结构化中间步骤的形式验证来增强LLM推理可靠性的奖励方法，在保持准确性的同时提高推理可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于结果奖励的强化学习虽然能提升LLM在复杂多步推理任务上的表现，但往往忽略有缺陷的中间步骤，导致即使最终答案正确，推理过程也不可靠。需要一种方法在保持准确性的同时增强推理可靠性。

Method: 提出PRoSFI（Process Reward over Structured Formal Intermediates）方法：模型输出与其自然语言推理对齐的结构化中间步骤，每个步骤由形式验证器进行验证，只有完全验证通过的推理链才能获得高奖励。这种方法引导模型生成可机器验证的逐步证明。

Result: PRoSFI提供了一种简单有效的训练可信推理模型的方法，能够在不损害准确性的前提下增强推理可靠性，特别是对于中等规模（7B）模型，避免了直接生成形式证明的困难。

Conclusion: 通过结构化中间步骤的形式验证来奖励推理过程，能够有效提升LLM推理的可信度，为解决结果奖励忽视中间步骤缺陷的问题提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have recently demonstrated impressive performance on complex, multi-step reasoning tasks, especially when post-trained with outcome-rewarded reinforcement learning Guo et al. 2025. However, it has been observed that outcome rewards often overlook flawed intermediate steps, leading to unreliable reasoning steps even when final answers are correct. To address this unreliable reasoning, we propose PRoSFI (Process Reward over Structured Formal Intermediates), a novel reward method that enhances reasoning reliability without compromising accuracy. Instead of generating formal proofs directly, which is rarely accomplishable for a modest-sized (7B) model, the model outputs structured intermediate steps aligned with its natural language reasoning. Each step is then verified by a formal prover. Only fully validated reasoning chains receive high rewards. The integration of formal verification guides the model towards generating step-by-step machine-checkable proofs, thereby yielding more credible final answers. PRoSFI offers a simple and effective approach to training trustworthy reasoning models.

</details>


### [58] [FlowPIE: Test-Time Scientific Idea Evolution with Flow-Guided Literature Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29557)
*Qiyao Wang,Hongbo Wang,Longze Chen,Zhihao Yang,Guhong Chen,Hamid Alinejad-Rokny,Hui Li,Yuan Lin,Min Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FlowPIE：一种紧密耦合的检索-生成框架，将文献探索与科学思想生成视为协同进化过程，通过流引导的MCTS和基于LLM的奖励模型指导自适应检索，再通过测试时思想进化过程生成多样高质量的科学思想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学思想生成方法受限于静态的检索-生成范式，导致思想同质化且发散性不足，无法有效突破信息茧房问题。

Method: 1. 流引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）进行文献轨迹扩展；2. 基于LLM的生成奖励模型评估思想质量；3. 自适应检索构建多样高质量初始种群；4. 测试时思想进化过程：选择、交叉、变异操作；5. 隔离岛屿范式结合跨领域知识。

Result: FlowPIE相比现有基于LLM和智能体的框架，能持续产生更高新颖性、可行性和多样性的科学思想，同时在测试时实现奖励缩放。

Conclusion: FlowPIE通过将文献探索与思想生成紧密耦合，有效缓解了过度依赖参数化知识和静态文献导致的信息茧房问题，为AI驱动的自主研究提供了更有效的科学思想生成框架。

Abstract: Scientific idea generation (SIG) is critical to AI-driven autonomous research, yet existing approaches are often constrained by a static retrieval-then-generation paradigm, leading to homogeneous and insufficiently divergent ideas. In this work, we propose FlowPIE, a tightly coupled retrieval-generation framework that treats literature exploration and idea generation as a co-evolving process. FlowPIE expands literature trajectories via a flow-guided Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) inspired by GFlowNets, using the quality of current ideas assessed by an LLM-based generative reward model (GRM) as a supervised signal to guide adaptive retrieval and construct a diverse, high-quality initial population. Based on this population, FlowPIE models idea generation as a test-time idea evolution process, applying selection, crossover, and mutation with the isolation island paradigm and GRM-based fitness computation to incorporate cross-domain knowledge. It effectively mitigates the information cocoons arising from over-reliance on parametric knowledge and static literature. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that FlowPIE consistently produces ideas with higher novelty, feasibility and diversity compared to strong LLM-based and agent-based frameworks, while enabling reward scaling during test time.

### [59] [ASI-Evolve: AI Accelerates AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29640)
*Weixian Xu,Tiantian Mi,Yixiu Liu,Yang Nan,Zhimeng Zhou,Lyumanshan Ye,Lin Zhang,Yu Qiao,Pengfei Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ASI-Evolve是一个AI-for-AI研究框架，通过认知基础和专用分析器实现学习-设计-实验-分析闭环，在神经网络架构、预训练数据策展和强化学习算法三个核心AI开发领域实现自主发现，性能超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统在快速反馈的明确任务上表现良好，但无法应对成本高昂、长期、弱监督的真实AI研究循环。需要开发能够加速AI自身发展的AI系统。

Method: ASI-Evolve框架包含两个关键组件：1) 认知基础：将积累的人类先验知识注入每轮探索；2) 专用分析器：将复杂实验结果提炼为可重用的见解。框架通过学习-设计-实验-分析循环实现AI-for-AI研究。

Result: 在神经网络架构设计中发现了105个SOTA线性注意力架构，最佳模型超越DeltaNet 0.97个点；预训练数据策展管道将平均基准性能提升3.96个点，MMLU上增益超18个点；强化学习算法设计在AMC32上超越GRPO 12.5个点，AIME24上11.67个点，OlympiadBench上5.04个点。

Conclusion: ASI-Evolve代表了AI加速AI发展的有前景的一步，提供了闭环AI研究可行性的早期证据，并展示了该范式在数学和生物医学等AI栈之外的迁移潜力。

Abstract: Can AI accelerate the development of AI itself? While recent agentic systems have shown strong performance on well-scoped tasks with rapid feedback, it remains unclear whether they can tackle the costly, long-horizon, and weakly supervised research loops that drive real AI progress. We present ASI-Evolve, an agentic framework for AI-for-AI research that closes this loop through a learn-design-experiment-analyze cycle. ASI-Evolve augments standard evolutionary agents with two key components: a cognition base that injects accumulated human priors into each round of exploration, and a dedicated analyzer that distills complex experimental outcomes into reusable insights for future iterations. To our knowledge, ASI-Evolve is the first unified framework to demonstrate AI-driven discovery across three central components of AI development: data, architectures, and learning algorithms. In neural architecture design, it discovered 105 SOTA linear attention architectures, with the best discovered model surpassing DeltaNet by +0.97 points, nearly 3x the gain of recent human-designed improvements. In pretraining data curation, the evolved pipeline improves average benchmark performance by +3.96 points, with gains exceeding 18 points on MMLU. In reinforcement learning algorithm design, discovered algorithms outperform GRPO by up to +12.5 points on AMC32, +11.67 points on AIME24, and +5.04 points on OlympiadBench. We further provide initial evidence that this AI-for-AI paradigm can transfer beyond the AI stack through experiments in mathematics and biomedicine. Together, these results suggest that ASI-Evolve represents a promising step toward enabling AI to accelerate AI across the foundational stages of development, offering early evidence for the feasibility of closed-loop AI research.

Conclusion: 该研究填补了多站点血液捐赠网络中捐赠者邀请调度的操作空白，提出的优化框架能够有效平衡捐赠者便利性、资格和血型需求。贪心算法在计算效率和内存使用方面具有显著优势，尽管在全局优化性能上略有妥协，为实际应用提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Blood donation centers face challenges in matching supply with demand while managing donor availability. Although targeted outreach is important, it can cause donor fatigue via over-solicitation. Effective recruitment requires targeting the right donors at the right time, balancing constraints with donor convenience and eligibility. Despite extensive work on blood supply chain optimization and growing interest in algorithmic donor recruitment, the operational problem of assigning donors to sessions across a multi-site network, taking into account eligibility, capacity, blood-type demand targets, geographic convenience, and donor safety, remains unaddressed.
  We address this gap with an optimization framework for donor invitation scheduling incorporating donor eligibility, travel convenience, blood-type demand targets, and penalties. We evaluate two strategies: (i) a binary integer linear programming (BILP) formulation and (ii) an efficient greedy heuristic. Evaluation uses the registry from Instituto Português do Sangue e da Transplantação (IPST) for invite planning in the Lisbon operational region using 4-month windows. A prospective pipeline integrates organic attendance forecasting, quantile-based demand targets, and residual capacity estimation for forward-looking invitation plans. Results reveal its key role in closing the supply-demand gap in the Lisbon operational region. A controlled comparison shows that the greedy heuristic achieves results comparable to the BILP, with 188x less peak memory and 115x faster runtime; trade-offs include 3.9 pp lower demand fulfillment (86.1% vs. 90.0%), larger donor-session distance, higher adverse-reaction donor exposure, and greater invitation burden per non-high-frequency donor, reflecting local versus global optimization. Experiments assess how constraint-aware scheduling can close gaps by mobilizing eligible inactive/lapsing donors.

### [61] [View-oriented Conversation Compiler for Agent Trace Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29678)
*Lvmin Zhang,Maneesh Agrawala*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: VCC编译器将原始代理JSONL日志转换为结构化视图，提升上下文学习分析质量，减少token消耗，提高通过率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代代理对话包含深层结构化内容（嵌套工具调用、思维链推理块、子代理调用等），远超简单用户-助手交换的复杂度。将此类跟踪以纯文本、JSON或YAML等形式馈送到分析机制会显著降低分析质量。需要专门的基础设施来处理代理对话的复杂性。

Method: 提出VCC（视图导向对话编译器），采用编译器架构（词法分析、语法分析、中间表示、降级、生成），将原始代理JSONL日志转换为三种结构化视图：完整视图（无损转录，作为规范行号坐标系）、用户界面视图（重构用户实际感知的交互）、自适应视图（由相关性谓词控制的结构保持投影）。

Result: 在AppWorld的上下文学习实验中，仅将反射器输入格式从原始JSONL替换为VCC编译视图，在所有三种测试模型配置中均获得更高通过率，同时将反射器token消耗减少一半到三分之二，并产生更简洁的学习记忆。

Conclusion: 消息格式应被视为上下文学习的基础设施，而非偶然的实现选择。VCC编译器通过结构化视图转换显著提升了代理跟踪分析的质量和效率。

Abstract: Agent traces carry increasing analytical value in the era of context learning and harness-driven agentic cognition, yet most prior work treats conversation format as a trivial engineering detail. Modern agent conversations contain deeply structured content, including nested tool calls and results, chain-of-thought reasoning blocks, sub-agent invocations, context-window compaction boundaries, and harness-injected system directives, whose complexity far exceeds that of simple user-assistant exchanges. Feeding such traces to a reflector or other analytical mechanism in plain text, JSON, YAML, or via grep can materially degrade analysis quality. This paper presents VCC (View-oriented Conversation Compiler), a compiler (lex, parse, IR, lower, emit) that transforms raw agent JSONL logs into a family of structured views: a full view (lossless transcript serving as the canonical line-number coordinate system), a user-interface view (reconstructing the interaction as the user actually perceived it), and an adaptive view (a structure-preserving projection governed by a relevance predicate). In a context-learning experiment on AppWorld, replacing only the reflector's input format, from raw JSONL to VCC-compiled views, leads to higher pass rates across all three model configurations tested, while cutting reflector token consumption by half to two-thirds and producing more concise learned memory. These results suggest that message format functions as infrastructure for context learning, not as an incidental implementation choice.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于生成式AI对认知影响的研究过于简化，特别是将AI使用与邓宁-克鲁格效应简单等同的观点无法解释复杂的实证证据。需要更精细的理论框架来解释AI如何同时改善任务表现却损害元认知能力。

Method: 综合人类-AI交互、学习研究和模型评估的证据，提出AI介导的元认知解耦工作模型，该模型包含四个变量：产出输出、底层理解、校准准确性和自我评估能力。

Abstract: The common claim that generative AI simply amplifies the Dunning-Kruger effect is too coarse to capture the available evidence. The clearest findings instead suggest that large language model (LLM) use can improve observable output and short-term task performance while degrading metacognitive accuracy and flattening the classic competence-confidence gradient across skill groups. This paper synthesizes evidence from human-AI interaction, learning research, and model evaluation, and proposes the working model of AI-mediated metacognitive decoupling: a widening gap among produced output, underlying understanding, calibration accuracy, and self-assessed ability. This four-variable account better explains overconfidence, over- and under-reliance, crutch effects, and weak transfer than the simpler metaphor of a uniformly steeper Dunning-Kruger curve. The paper concludes with implications for tool design, assessment, and knowledge work.

### [63] [A First Step Towards Even More Sparse Encodings of Probability Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29691)
*Florian Andreas Marwitz,Tanya Braun,Ralf Möller*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出从概率分布中提取一阶逻辑公式的方法，通过减少分布中的值数量并为每个值提取逻辑公式进行最小化，从而增加编码稀疏性并泛化分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界场景可以用提升概率分布表示，但传统编码方式（表格或列表）需要指数级数量的值，导致表示效率低下。

Method: 通过减少概率分布中的值数量，为每个值提取逻辑公式，然后对公式进行最小化处理，从而获得稀疏编码表示。

Result: 评估显示，通过提取少量简短公式可以极大增加稀疏性，同时保留核心信息。

Conclusion: 该方法能够显著减少概率分布编码所需的值数量，通过提取最小化的一阶逻辑公式实现高效稀疏表示。

Abstract: Real world scenarios can be captured with lifted probability distributions. However, distributions are usually encoded in a table or list, requiring an exponential number of values. Hence, we propose a method for extracting first-order formulas from probability distributions that require significantly less values by reducing the number of values in a distribution and then extracting, for each value, a logical formula to be further minimized. This reduction and minimization allows for increasing the sparsity in the encoding while also generalizing a given distribution. Our evaluation shows that sparsity can increase immensely by extracting a small set of short formulas while preserving core information.

### [64] [Measuring the metacognition of AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29693)
*Richard Servajean,Philippe Servajean*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出采用meta-d'框架及其无模型替代方案作为评估AI元认知敏感性的黄金标准，并利用信号检测理论测量AI基于不确定性和风险自发调节决策的能力，通过LLM实验验证了这些心理物理学框架的实用性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出采用meta-d'框架及其无模型替代方案作为评估AI元认知敏感性的黄金标准，并利用信号检测理论测量AI基于不确定性和风险自发调节决策的能力。通过两个系列实验在三个大型语言模型上进行验证：第一个实验中LLMs执行主要判断后提供置信度评级；第二个实验中LLMs仅执行主要判断，同时操纵与响应相关的风险。

Result: 应用meta-d'框架可以在三个维度进行比较：将LLM与最优性比较、在不同LLM之间比较、在同一LLM的不同任务间比较。信号检测理论能够评估LLMs在高风险情况下是否变得更加保守。实验验证了这些心理物理学框架在评估AI元认知能力方面的实用性。

Conclusion: meta-d'框架和信号检测理论为评估AI系统的元认知能力提供了稳健的方法论框架，有助于系统测量AI在不确定性和风险条件下的决策质量调节能力，对AI系统集成到决策工作流程具有重要意义。

Abstract: A robust decision-making process must take into account uncertainty, especially when the choice involves inherent risks. Because artificial Intelligence (AI) systems are increasingly integrated into decision-making workflows, managing uncertainty relies more and more on the metacognitive capabilities of these systems; i.e, their ability to assess the reliability of and regulate their own decisions. Hence, it is crucial to employ robust methods to measure the metacognitive abilities of AI. This paper is primarily a methodological contribution arguing for the adoption of the meta-d' framework, or its model-free alternatives, as the gold standard for assessing the metacognitive sensitivity of AIs--the ability to generate confidence ratings that distinguish correct from incorrect responses. Moreover, we propose to leverage signal detection theory (SDT) to measure the ability of AIs to spontaneously regulate their decisions based on uncertainty and risk. To demonstrate the practical utility of these psychophysical frameworks, we conduct two series of experiments on three large language models (LLMs)--GPT-5, DeepSeek-V3.2-Exp, and Mistral-Medium-2508. In the first experiments, LLMs performed a primary judgment followed by a confidence rating. In the second, LLMs only performed the primary judgment, while we manipulated the risk associated with either response. On the one hand, applying the meta-d' framework allows us to conduct comparisons along three axes: comparing an LLM to optimality, comparing different LLMs on a given task, and comparing the same LLM across different tasks. On the other hand, SDT allows us to assess whether LLMs become more conservative when risks are high.

### [65] [Symphony for Medical Coding: A Next-Generation Agentic System for Scalable and Explainable Medical Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29709)
*Joakim Edin,Andreas Motzfeldt,Simon Flachs,Lars Maaløe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Symphony是一个基于推理的医疗编码系统，通过直接访问编码指南来模拟专家编码员的工作方式，支持跨编码系统并提供证据链接，在多个真实数据集上达到SOTA性能。

Method: Symphony系统模拟专家编码员的工作方式：通过直接访问编码指南对临床叙述进行推理。该系统设计允许跨任何编码系统操作，并提供跨度级别的证据，将每个预测代码链接到支持它的文本。

Result: 在两个公共基准和三个真实世界数据集上评估，涵盖美国和美国住院、门诊、急诊和专科设置。Symphony在所有设置中都达到了最先进的结果，证明其作为自动化临床编码的灵活、可部署基础。

Conclusion: Symphony通过模拟人类专家编码员的推理过程，解决了现有自动化医疗编码系统的关键限制，提供了一个灵活、可解释且可跨编码系统部署的解决方案，为自动化临床编码奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Medical coding translates free-text clinical documentation into standardized codes drawn from classification systems that contain tens of thousands of entries and are updated annually. It is central to billing, clinical research, and quality reporting, yet remains largely manual, slow, and error-prone. Existing automated approaches learn to predict a fixed set of codes from labeled data, thereby preventing adaptation to new codes or different coding systems without retraining on different data. They also provide no explanation for their predictions, limiting trust in safety-critical settings. We introduce Symphony for Medical Coding, a system that approaches the task the way expert human coders do: by reasoning over the clinical narrative with direct access to the coding guidelines. This design allows Symphony to operate across any coding system and to provide span-level evidence linking each predicted code to the text that supports it. We evaluate on two public benchmarks and three real-world datasets spanning inpatient, outpatient, emergency, and subspecialty settings across the United States and the United Kingdom. Symphony achieves state-of-the-art results across all settings, establishing itself as a flexible, deployment-ready foundation for automated clinical coding.

### [69] [Tracking vs. Deciding: The Dual-Capability Bottleneck in Searchless Chess Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29761)
*Quanhao Li,Wei Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个类人国际象棋引擎，通过序列训练学习状态跟踪和决策质量两种能力，采用参数扩展和Elo加权训练解决两种能力的数据需求矛盾，最终模型在无搜索情况下达到Lichess子弹棋2570等级分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一个类人的国际象棋引擎，能够模仿人类棋手的风格、错误和一致性，而不是单纯追求最大化的棋力。传统方法面临状态跟踪和决策质量两种能力的数据需求矛盾：低等级对局提供状态跟踪所需的多样性，高等级对局提供决策学习所需的质量信号。

Method: 1. 从移动序列训练模型，强制学习状态跟踪（从历史走法重建棋盘）和决策质量（从重建状态选择好着法）两种能力；2. 形式化为双能力瓶颈P≤min(T,Q)；3. 将模型参数从28M扩展到120M以改善状态跟踪；4. 引入Elo加权训练以改善决策质量同时保持多样性；5. 使用2×2因子消融实验验证效果；6. 提出覆盖衰减公式t*=log(N/kcrit)/log b作为可靠性视野。

Result: 最终120M参数模型在无搜索情况下达到Lichess子弹棋2570等级分（253局评级对局）。在人类着法预测任务上达到55.2% Top-1准确率，超过Maia-2快速棋和Maia-2闪电棋模型。序列输入自然编码完整对局历史，能够实现单局面模型无法展现的历史依赖决策。

Conclusion: 类人国际象棋引擎需要平衡状态跟踪和决策质量两种能力，通过参数扩展和Elo加权训练可以协同提升两种能力。序列训练方法能够自然编码完整对局历史，实现历史依赖的决策，为开发更类人的AI棋手提供了有效途径。

Abstract: A human-like chess engine should mimic the style, errors, and consistency of a strong human player rather than maximize playing strength. We show that training from move sequences alone forces a model to learn two capabilities: state tracking, which reconstructs the board from move history, and decision quality, which selects good moves from that reconstructed state. These impose contradictory data requirements: low-rated games provide the diversity needed for tracking, while high-rated games provide the quality signal for decision learning. Removing low-rated data degrades performance.
  We formalize this tension as a dual-capability bottleneck, P <= min(T,Q), where overall performance is limited by the weaker capability. Guided by this view, we scale the model from 28M to 120M parameters to improve tracking, then introduce Elo-weighted training to improve decisions while preserving diversity. A 2 x 2 factorial ablation shows that scaling improves tracking, weighting improves decisions, and their combination is superadditive. Linear weighting works best, while overly aggressive weighting harms tracking despite lower validation loss. We also introduce a coverage-decay formula, t* = log(N/kcrit)/log b, as a reliability horizon for intra-game degeneration risk.
  Our final 120M-parameter model, without search, reached Lichess bullet 2570 over 253 rated games. On human move prediction it achieves 55.2% Top-1 accuracy, exceeding Maia-2 rapid and Maia-2 blitz. Unlike position-based methods, sequence input naturally encodes full game history, enabling history-dependent decisions that single-position models cannot exhibit.
